Build 2026 Podcast: Satya Nadella, Sarah Guo and Elad Gil from No Priors, and Swyx from Latent Space

Microsoft(2.2M) ·41:05 ·2.4K views · 2026-06-04
Satya Nadella (CEO, Microsoft) Sarah Guo (Co-host, No Priors) Elad Gil (Co-host, No Priors)
AI value is shifting from raw foundation models to an ecosystem-driven "harness" layer where enterprises use private evaluations and custom agentic workflows to hill-climb performance.
TL;DR AI value is shifting from raw foundation models to an ecosystem-driven "harness" layer where enterprises use private evaluations and custom agentic workflows to hill-climb performance. To capture compounding value, organizations must transition from manual execution to...

TL;DR

AI value is shifting from raw foundation models to an ecosystem-driven "harness" layer where enterprises use private evaluations and custom agentic workflows to hill-climb performance. To capture compounding value, organizations must transition from manual execution to "meta-work"—building autonomous systems that capture institutional tacit knowledge directly onto the corporate balance sheet.

## The Platform Shift: From Foundation Models to "Harnesses"

  • Defining the Platform: True platforms must create more economic value *above* the platform layer than they capture within it. Microsoft's primary objective is to enable all companies—from AI-native startups to legacy enterprises—to operate at the cognitive frontier with their own data and "frontier intelligence."
  • The Rise of the Harness: The core engineering challenge has shifted from model training to building the "harness"—the integrated loop linking models, context, and developer tools.
      • Open and Multi-Model Harnessing: Microsoft encourages open harnesses (such as supporting Meta's Llama alongside proprietary models) to give developers architectural flexibility.
      • The Land O'Lakes Playbook: A key design pattern involves using a frontier model (like GPT-4) to collect process traces, and then utilizing a smaller reasoning model (like Phi-3) to execute the task at a higher performance-to-cost ratio.
  • Private Evals as Definitive IP: Standard public benchmarks are easily maxed out and do not reflect real-world business utility. A company's private evaluation suite is its most critical intellectual property.
      • Model Portability: If an enterprise can swap Model A for Model B using their private evals and continue to "hill climb" performance, they retain strategic control. If they cannot swap models, they are locked into a vendor.
      • Clean Lineage Models: Microsoft's MAI models focus heavily on pre-training data quality and rigorous ablations to avoid the common pitfall of open-weight models that benchmark well but fail in production.

## Unbundling SaaS and the "Balance Sheet" AI Agent

  • Deconstructing the SaaS Stack: Traditional SaaS applications bundle a data model, business logic, and UI. AI is unbundling this vertical stack. While UI will change completely, foundational data schemas (like a general ledger) and business logic (like Power BI semantic models) remain highly valuable databases for feeding agents.
  • M365 and Work IQ as an Enterprise Database: Microsoft 365 is transitioning from a suite of captive applications into an accessible enterprise database.
      • Cross-Domain Workflows: Through Work IQ, an agent can analyze Microsoft Teams design meeting transcripts from the prior week and automatically generate a plan to modify a codebase inside a GitHub repository.
  • Putting Tacit Knowledge on the Balance Sheet: Human capital and institutional experience have historically been impossible to list as physical assets. By capturing the traces of long-running agentic workflows, companies can build "veteran agents" that preserve tacit knowledge. This operational capability will eventually be recognized as balance sheet value.
  • Business Model Adaptations: While per-user subscriptions will persist due to corporate budget predictability, consumption-based pricing is growing to accommodate high-intensity, background agent workloads. GitHub, for instance, adjusted its pricing models to account for the heavy token usage of autonomous agent sessions compared to simple interactive autocomplete.

## Meta-Work, Generalist Leverage, and the Future of Engineering

  • The Pivot to Meta-Work: High organizational ambition in the AI era requires shifting human roles from performing a task to building the agentic system that executes it.
      • Azure's "Miles" System: To handle massive scaling—building more Azure capacity in 15 months than in the prior 15 years—the Azure networking team built an agentic system named *Miles* to manage physical wide-area network (WAN) fiber operations. The team successfully scaled operations by requesting "tokens over headcount."
  • Consolidation of Engineering Roles: Engineering is consolidating around high-leverage disciplines.
      • Full-Stack Builders: Teams at LinkedIn are merging product management, design, and front-end engineering into unified "Full-Stack Builder" roles.
      • Specialized Infrastructure: Demand is rising for distributed systems engineers to build reward systems (RLHF/RLAIF) for specialized applications, such as Microsoft Excel's underlying logic.
  • Satya's Chief of Staff Agent: Highlighting the democratization of software building, Satya Nadella built a personal "Chief of Staff" Autopilot. He utilized Work IQ to create a long-running Foundry agent, stored its memory in Rayfin (backend-as-a-service), and successfully published the functional application to Microsoft Teams.

## Hyper-Scale Infrastructure and Earning "Community Permission"

  • Redefining the Hyperscaler: The sheer scale of data center buildouts is unprecedented, fundamentally shifting the capital requirements and physical footprint of technology providers.
  • Earning Community Permission: Tech companies cannot rely on "trust us" narratives regarding AI's future benefits. They must deliver immediate, tangible value to the local communities hosting data centers.
      • Resource and Infrastructure Co-Investment: Data centers must actively improve the local energy grid, replenish local water supplies through closed-loop systems, and expand the local tax base via construction and long-term operational jobs.
  • A New Pedagogy for Education: AI's ability to lower the friction of information retrieval demands a redesign of educational credentials and continuous learning. Nadella suggests that the next generation of breakout startups could include entirely new universities built around AI-driven training and economic opportunity placement.

## Notable Quotes

"A platform is defined by, fundamentally, its ability to create more value above the platform versus what's captured in the platform." — Satya Nadella
"Every company having private evals may be the biggest IP... If you have an eval that's private, you're using a model A, can you switch it to model B and climb up? If you can, then you're in control. If you can't, you're not in control." — Satya Nadella
"Our job is not to do Azure networking, our job is to build the agentic system that does Azure networking... They basically took their work and made it meta." — Satya Nadella
"The world is going to be way skeptical of tech and tech companies that say, 'Trust us, we've got it. The future is going to be glorious.' You kind of have to deliver tangible benefits." — Satya Nadella
Please welcome Swyx, Sarah Guo, Elad Gil, and Chairman and Chief Executive Officer of Microsoft, Satya Nadella. Hello, Swyx. I'm so excited to be here. Welcome to a crossover episode of No Priors and Latent Space with Satya Nadella. Congratulations on an amazing Build. No, thank you so much and it's great to be with both of you. I, I'd say there are, perhaps the, the biggest one for me is, let's sort of conceptualize this more as an ecosystem play as opposed to a single model or even a single platform, right?
